### Post by hadriansong on 2013-12-12
Hello. I am a newbie just started to study Kernel programming.
I am trying to add certain syscall to my kernel and I followed several examples that show how to add syscall. 
I successfully compiled my kernel but whenever I make userprogram to check the syscall i added, it keeps giving me return value -1, which means there are some errors.

Here is links that i followed.
[http://impact.asu.edu/cse430fa12/CSE430%20FA%202012%20-%20HW2.pdf](http://impact.asu.edu/cse430fa12/CSE430%20FA%202012%20-%20HW2.pdf)
[http://arvindsraj.wordpress.com/2012/10/05/adding-hello-world-system-call-to-linux/](http://arvindsraj.wordpress.com/2012/10/05/adding-hello-world-system-call-to-linux/)

I just have no idea, why i am getting this value. 

I thought whenever I complie my kernel, it will update the user mode as well.
